holy chirche vnyed ſayd loue yt holy gooſt euery man hath parte goodnes well heuen alſo erthe ſayntes paradyſe reioyſe good werkes merytoryous yt whiche done vpon erthe theſe faythfull cryſtē men tymes founde experyence whiche foloweth yeres thouſande foure hondred foure ſcore thre noble man royalme fraunce vnto gooſtly fader reknowleged confeſſed vpon loyalte fayth pleated thre yeres grande grete aſſyſe cyte bourgeys ryght belened haue thre halfe pen rente yere yet fyne ende cauſe abode doubte leſe wynne affermed coſtes dyſpenſes well moeuable herytage hath taken beſte counſeyll vnto hym merueylous dyfferrence bytwene eſtate dedely ſynne eſtate grace ſtondynge ſynner hath many ſynnes aſmoche hym ought enforce good werkes often preſeruyd fall ſynnes alſo hym dyſpoſeth ableth contynue good werkes lyfe vertuous alſo yf ſuche vnto hym haue ben enioyned penaūce hym acquyteth penaunce mooſt hole opynyon alſo occupyeth tyme fruytfully hym maketh ſom takynge parte theſe good perſones alſo auoydeth paynes temporall whiche oftymes comen cauſe ſynnes deſerueth agayne grete lyberalyte god proſperyte godes tēporall alſo letten ye deuyll yt hath ſo grete puyſſaūce noye ye ſynner alſo releſen ye paynes hell purgatory y• knowe yt man ſhall beſo moche punyſſhed ſuch tyme yt man ſhold ſuche good dedes hath ben ydell prouoken mercy dyuyne gyue grace y• whiche man may go ſȳne yf ſuche perſones fynably ſaued ſhall haue ioye eternall thoſe goodneſſes done eſtate dedely ſynne ſuche ſoo greate yf hadde theym done eſtate grace good werkes done ye loue god ſtere put knocke yate mercy dyuyne ſayd goſpell mater declareth ryght longe ſaynt bernardyn thre ſcore foure ſermon ſomme whiche intytled de contracti bus ¶here foloweth vi reaſons ſhewynge ſinner ne ought tary hym confeſſe fyrſt reaſon wherfore man ought caplm v tary hym confeſſe condycyon ſynne lyke vnto fyre brēnynge whyche may quenched trewe cōfeſſyon whiche ought haue abundaunce teerys leeſt ſpyrytuell whiche ben ſorowe dyſpleaſure haue offended god ſynne lyke wyſe ſholde holden fole whiche ſeeth houſe brennynge may remedye caſtynge water nothynge wyl ſoo whiche ben dedely ſynne putteth theyr dylygence purge trewe confeſſyon ſeconde moche ſynne ryght perylous ſykneſſe confeſſyon ryght certayne medycyne proufytable whiche apperyth full fewe preyſe helthe theyr ſoule whiche ſeeth hym ſelfe ſyke nere deed obe ye without fermynge conſcyence erronyous yf partye beleueth dedely ſynne obeye partye dede maryage tyme grete ſolempnyte neuertheleſſe notwithſtandynge hym ſhe obeyeth ſhe ſynneth mortally alonely moche ſhe dooth contrary conſcyence whiche erronyous byleue obeye partye ſayd tyme dedely ſynne vi whan werke maryage commytted place halowed chirche chirchyerde yf theſe partyes maryed may otherwyſe incontynence dyſpoſe vnto ſuche pareyl ſynnen mortally ſome doctours vn purpoſe haue founde tymes man maryed ſorowe remors conſcyence ſought remedy counſeyll wyfe hath hadde foure fyue chyldern deed practyſe ought holde whiche entyerly hym wyll confeſſe examen order x commaundementes lawe mooſte ſure maner may founde ſo euer wyll well parfaytly examē caplm xiiii conſcyence partyculer ought rule hym x commaundementes lawe ſo wytneſſeth ſaynt auſten man may fynde certayne practyſe examen well conſcyence alſo ſayth well ſaynt gregorye x commaundementes ben ten myrrours whiche ſoule cryſtened may clerely ſee knowe fylth ſynne dyſordynaunce conſcyence alſo ſayth ryall prophete dauyd ſhall confeſſe well ryghtly moche haue lerned ten commaūdementes god whiche well noted perſone bounde hym confeſſe regulerly neceſſyte onely dedely ſynne whiche thynge tranſgreſſyon ony x cōmaundementes whiche ben defended ſeuen deedly ſynnes alſo conteyned ſeuen werkes mercy trouth artycles oure holy fayth y• whiche thynges vnderſtonde commaundementes lawe artycles fayth ſeuen werkes mercy comprehended cōteyned dede conſcyence lyke wyſe hath ben ſayd therfore ſo euer wyll hym well examen make parfyte hole confeſſyon theſe thynges ſayd ought take hede hath kepte accō plyſſhed ten cōmaundementes god well thynge cōmaunded ſechynge vertues accomplyſſhynge werkes mercy alſo thynge defended ben ſeuen dedely ſynnes know pryde enuy wrath couetyſe glotonye ſlouth lechery y• whiche ſeuen maner ſynnes man may falle often mortally dampnably ſomtyme venyall alonely byleue euery paſſyon mouynge ire enuy vayne glorye ſoo ſynnes ſayd ben alwayes deedly ſynne whan ſuche paſſyons wylles abyden termes venyall ſynne exceden tyll vnto mortall ſynne thynge ryght harde vnto jugement humayne poſſyble therin gyue rule generall ſuffycyent juge euery caſe inpartyculer wheder mortall venyall hath ben ſayd ſeuenth chapytre partye therfore nowe reſte ſee partyculer ſome caſe y• ordre ten cōmaundementes ¶here foloweth fyrſte commaundement ouer theſe thynges ſayd fyrſte cōmaundement caplm xv whiche wyll well purge cō ſcyence ought take hede vnto theſe poyntes folowen fyrſte vnto brekynge vowes yf ony haue ben broken ſayth carynge dyſpyſynge inobedyence agayne god whiche lawfull holde accomplyſſhe dedely ſynne yf man cōmytte ſuche fraccy delyberacyon equyualente rule put chapytre ſcyence confeſſour ought haue whiche oughte well noted theſe caſes whiche folowen mater ten commaundementes alſo noted moche hath ben made mencyon treatyſe cōmaundemen te ſeuen deedly ſynnes whiche ſtudye boke wyll examen conſeyence ought truſte thynges whiche hath ben ſayd generall eſpecyall folowen recapitulacy cōmaundementes partyculer yf ony ſyknes forgetfulnes cauſe excuſable breketh hys vowe ſynne alonely venyall yf hath auowed thynge vnlefull ne ſholde accomplyſſhe without dyſpenſe ought ſooner contrary hym confeſſe ſoo folyſſhely haue auowed thynge whiche lefull honeſte yf haue taryed accomplyſſhe vowes ſuche wyſe thē hath forgoten moche taryenge falleth ſuche inconuenyent ne may accomplyſſhe ſome grete theologyens wyll ſaye ſuſteyne yt deedly ſynne yf haue made auowe faſte thynge lefull ony curſyd ende come cōmytte thefte auoutry ſynne hath ſynned mortally yf hath made auowe chaſtyte relegyon afterwarde hym maryeth deedly ſynne many tymes often requyreth partye deuoure maryage ſynneth mortally yf requyred may acquyte hym yeldynge deuoyre maryage without deedly ſynne ſuche wyſe loueth better wyll reaſon hym content accomplyſſhe werke maryage whiche thynge yl kepe tyme lyfe therfore yt ben ſuche inconuenyent ſholde make dyſpenſe theyr vowe aſſoyled ſynne noted curate may aſſoyle ſubiecte brekynge vowes may dyſpence chaunge without ſpecyall lycence pope byſſhop caſe requyreth dyſpenſacyon cōmutacyon vowe chaſtyte pylgrymage vnto jheruſalem rome ſaynt james ben reſerued pope dyſpence commutacyons vowes appertayne vnto prelate alſo noted yonge people knowe ye doughter vnder yeres xii accomplyſſhed ſone vnder yeres xiiii may vowe entre relegyon theyr owne auctoryte withſtondynge dyſcrecyon ſo euer may haue alſo auowe oblygatory yf made delyberacyon full conſent alſo woman maryed may vowe obſerue vowe yt ſhe hath made maryage yf huſbond wyll ſo conſent yf ſhe hath auowed maryage huſbonde may make leue without dyſpenſe withoute ſynne ye one yf y• huſbonde ony tyme conſentynge man may well vowe without lycence partye whiche vnto preiudyce maryage alſo whiche vowen neuer kembe fryday ſpynne ſatyrdaye ſemblables ſuperſtytucyons ought leue ſuche vowes ſymple full vanytees doo ordenaunce theyr wyſe dyſcrete confeſſour holy faders secondly ſynner oughte well take hede yf culpable ſorceryes wytchcraftes charmes inuocacyons deuyll adoracyons paccyon hym dyabolykes alſo yf yt haue vſed ony euyll crafte yf haue kepte retayned bokes ſame alſo yf haue jugyd deth lyfe aduentures ony perſone conſtellacyons knowlege planettes ſkye phyloſephye alſo yf y• haue vſed ſorte knowe ony thynge yf hath byleued ouer moche ſtedfaſtly aduentures ony dremes yf hath lokyd cauſyd loke token hande knowe aduentures hymſelf yf ony ſyknes hath vſed lytell ſcrowes charmes yf hath put dyſtyncyon certayne dayes teweſdaye wēnyſdaye dayes begynne ony werke make waye beleuynge one daye ſhall profyte better nother yf hath put fayth ony aduentures ſonge cryes ony byrdes metynge ony beeſtes thynges theſe caſes ſayd oftymes dedely ſynne ryght ſelden venyall ſynne ¶here foloweth ſeconde commaundement theſe thynges ſayd ſeconde caplm xvi commaundement ſynner onght take hede vnto poyntes whiche folowen yf hath ſworne certayne thynge whiche doubte mortall ſynne ſpecyally jugemente yf hath ſworne thynge whiche ſelfe yll ſholde ſynne hath ſynned mortally ſuche othe ought kepte accomplyſſhed yf hath ſhewed wyttyngly ſecrete counſeyll hath ſworne holde ſecrete dedely ſynne well hym ſwereth hym whiche wyttyngly maketh ſuche reuelacyon knowynge well gyuen hym kepe ſecrete yf hath ſworne deteſtably ye blode yt deth wombe lorde dedely ſynne ſuche maner ſwere reputyd alſo blaſpheme lyke wyſe dyſpleaſe ire god ſayntes yf hath promyſed ſworne ony thynge deedly ſynne yf hath lente vpon gage thynge moeuable alſo herytage ſuche condycyon pryncypall intencyon ſhall haue vſage fruytes leue ſayd charge without deductynge rebaytynge ſomme lente vſury excepte gendred kynnyſman whiche taketh ony wage attendynge promyſſe whiche vnto hym hath ben made cauſe maryage wyfe ſuche wyſe mayntene huſbonde ought mayntene eſpouſe well notyd mater ben two maners vſuryes one clerely open ſayd hyd commytte dyuers maners yf hath bought londes poſſeſſyons lytyll mynyſſheth pryce moche ſeller putteth bargayne may bye agayne herytage wt certayne tyme cōmytteth vſurye yf rebate hath receyued ouer coſtes layenges ye ſayd herytage yf ſell many tymes harder leneth abaytynge payment tyll vnto certayne tyme ſome may ſewe ſpecyally whan loueth better haue vpon ower leſſe pryce tarye alſo whan hath bought certaȳ ware corne wyne whiche ben yet gadre moche hath auauncyd yc payment gyueth leſſe thynge worthe ower tyme ſholde receyue vſery alſo whan leneth pryncypally intencyon haue preſentes money ayde thynge temporall vſurye yf hath betaken beſtyall vnto haluys ſuche condycyon yt yf happen mortallyte aduenture loſſe wherof whiche taken cauſe neuertheles catyll ſhal euer ſauf entyer vſury rewle generall alwayes ſuche contractys ſhepe lā be hyre ox beſtes one partyes maketh pryce paccyon ſuche maner aſſured wynne nothynge leſe ſo euer happen partye abydeth doubte ſubiecte aduentures fortune ſuche cōtracte agayn reaſon agayne juſtyce whan exces one partye ſuche greate payne may loſſe gayns ſoo yt entende fraude one vnto put euery awayte vnto owne proffyte none vſurye yf procurer tuter ony faderles chyldern gyueth theyr fynaūce vnto vſury ende yt ſayd fynaūce vnto ſhall prouffyte meane nouryſſhed theyr maryages augmented alſo poore marchaundes ſuche meane myght auantage notwithſtondynge ſholde deedly ſynne ſayd procuroure tutour bounde reſtore ſayd vſurye caſe yf whiche haue hadde prouffyte wyll reſtore lyke wyſe ben dammage renneth whiche lended cauſe ſayd redy example grete requeſt lende hondred crownes yere whiche god good conſcyence ſhall dammage ſomme ten twenty crownes yf whiche borowed ſeeth ſholde better tymes valour tyme hyre hyre receyue man hath lente ony maner wyſe hath ben ſayd done ayenſt cōmaundement man ſelleth thynge imprecyable whiche proprely may ſolde vnderſtande pleaſure charyte euery creature ought vnto neyghbour well ye lawe nature lawe holy ſcrypture whiche lawes ben canon cyuyles defenden ye ſynne vſurye alſo yf ony gyne olde corne thynge ſemblable renewe hauynge intencyon pryncypall newe ſhall worth elles wolde gyue cōmytted vſurye yf pryncypally intente thynge peryſſhe pleaſure vnto neyghbour trewe ſemblable doubte yf thynge worthy leſſe tyme ſhall yelded agayne ſuche caas none vſurye payne vſurers publyſſhed ſuche ben excōmunycate ryght wherfore holy chirche defended vnto ſuche gyuen precyous body jheſu cryſte alſo theyr oblacyon receyued holy chirche alſo theyr deth theyr bodyes ben caſt voyde grounde receyued place holy bleſſyd man ought doubte ſoules theym whiche deyen ſuche eſtate ben dampned deuylles helle wherfore bodyes ſholde put reſte faythfull cryſten men yf theyr laſte dayes requyre penaunce may aſſoyled doynge yt yt poſſyble reſtore theſe vſuryes yt haue receyued theyr lyf ſuffyſed receyued vnto ye ſacramentꝭ holy chirche aſſoyled orden theyr teſtament yt theyr dethes theſe vſuryes ben reſtored behoued dyſpoſe mouable herytage tyll vnto ye ſomme whiche may amoūte ſayd vſuryes yf vnto whome ought make reſtytucōn ben preſent hȳ behoued make full ſatyſfaccion yeldynge fynaūce maruell gage aſſygnacōn yf ben abſent ye juge ye court lyuetenaūt ye byſſhop deane curate ſholden repreſent ye perſones receyuynge ſayd ſatyſfaccyon caas yt mouables herytagꝭ ſuffyſe not▪ often happened yt haue layde mouables herytages ſayd ſholde requyre mercy god holy chirche vnto whome ben redyuables man may aſſoyle elles teſtament make ony maner wyſe valour effecte ryght vnto peryll bounden wyues childern neuewes nyces enherytoures whiche wyttyngly retaynen goodes mouables herytages vſurers whiche haue made theyr lyf ſuffycyent reſtytucyon ſatyſfaccyon ought reſtored yf poſſyble oonly ſomme hath ben receyued vſurye dāmage myght haue hadde cauſe theym whiche haue payed ſayd vſuryes whiche apyreth clerely full fewe vſurers eſcapen deuyll lyke wyſe alſo appyreth peryll thoſe y• whiche receyuen theyr chirches chircheyerdes vnto ſepulture body vſurer ſuche hath ben ſpoken preeſtes whiche wyttyngly ben excōmunycate ipſo facto newe ryght alſo noted whiche taketh vnto vſurye grete neceſſyte hym whiche vſurer renommed redy ſynned takynge vnto vſurye take vnto vſurye auaryce dyſpende folyſſhely enduce ony gyue vnto vſurye whiche hath accuſtomed ſynne moche greuous ſhortely vnto ſeconde poynt ¶ foloweth fraude decepcyon vnto thyrde poynt whiche fraudes decepcyons whiche cōmytted dyuers maners people dyuers maners ſynner ſholde take hede fyrſte dede marchaundyſe ouer thynges ſayd vſurye yf hath done fraude fals weyghtes ony fals meſures ſellynge ony fals thynge corrupte meddled affermynge good pure metalles appotecaryes wyne oyle ony ware whiche byer notably defrauded deedly ſynne ſyns lytell thynge venyall ſynne well noted yf ony man defraude dyſceyued neyghbour lytell thynge hym wolde well dyſceyue greter thynge yf myght ſuche ſynnen mortally god ſeeth weyeth good wyll werke withoutforth hath frauded reteyned tax ſerches paſſages impoſicyons made ordynaūce juſtyce deedly ſynne alſo yf people ſeygnourye juſtyce haue made preſtes tax impoſicyons auaryce tyrannye comen wele mortall ſynne alſo yf hath falſed bookes receyte lettres vnto notable dāmage deedly ſynne alſo yf marchaūt marchaūdyſe pryncypally auaryce encreaſe catell lyue honeſtly vocacyon ayde poore welth comunalte deedly ſynne whan ſuche gayns putteth pryncypall entente yf ony bye ſtuffe ware intencyon ſelle agayne derer without chaungynge doynge ony crafte corne wyne ſholde waye wryte wood make ony crafte ſelle without caryenge one regyon comon welth pryncypally ſecheth ſuche maner encreaſe catell ſuche marchaundyſe vnlawfull may haue deedly ſynne ſayth mayſter fraūces de maronis alſo yf haue made paccyon bytwene ſelle theyr ware rudely pryce competent whiche comons conſtayned bye theyr pryce deedly ſynne alſo yf payed one ware whiche ſeynge hath aboue made owne mynyſſeth hurteth mortally deedly ſynne alſo yf hath payed ſymple people fals moneye fraude decepcyon deedly ſynne alſo yf hath vſed flaterynge ſpeche ſwerynges ſelle indyfferently daye feſte cōmaunded halowed place often deedly ſynne alſo yf hath bought robber theues byleued thynge ſuche apperteyned vnto juſtely deedly ſynne alſo yf hath ben meane ony co • tracte byleued vniuſte vſurye byenge herytage corſynge hors treatynge maryage ſeynge knowynge greuous dāmage one partyes deedly ſynne theſe thynges beforſayd vocacyon eſtate marchaundyſe man may applye vnto labourer handcrafty men ben draper taylers cordeners weuers tauerners baker pye baker ſmethes carpenter maſſons golſmithes labourer wt theyr armes labourer erthe euery vocacyon may fraude trechery malyce theyr werke weyght meſure valour intencyon theſe circumſtaūces yf god purenes conſcyence ne adreſſe therfore ſholde conſyder theyr eſtate occupacyons well ayde theyr confeſſour declare fraudes knowen well ſpeke ſubtylly y• clerke wrytynge may declare ſhold telle wheder leue ſuche maners fraudes ſhewe confeſſe playnly yf haue intencyon retorne cōtynuynge theyr dyſceyuable maners vſe ne ought aſſoyled alſo yf ony hym medle offyce crafte whiche may without deedly ſynne houſe ſteues ſyde ſeruyce vnto theſe vſurers meue warre whiche juſte make theſe mixions wherwt woman paynte theyr vyſages ſo vocacyons ſuche ought aſſoyled yf haue wyll neuer retorne vnto ſayd offyce alſo people y• whiche geten theyr journey faynen ſparen werke y• whiche euyll wyſe done theyr werke yt notwithſtandynge wyll well payed ben theues boūde make reſtytucyon example haue promyſſe xij pen journey put yt man thynketh ſuffycyent god good cōſcyence gete x pen moche theyr journeye lawfully ben theues ij pen vpon journeye ye amoūted ende yere yt man hath made cc ſuche journey ye ſomme xvi • viij whiche ſomme ought make reſtitucyon oftyme happened y• jugement god yt vnto ſuche people theyr goodes encreaſe yet profyten ſome dyſpende tauernes vnto cometh loſſes dāmages ye whiche fallen neceſſyte pouerte power reſtore yt whiche ſholde wel reaſon ſuche meane ben deceyued deuyll without nombre ſo ayded confeſſours ignorauntes whiche aſſoylen ſu che people without enioynynge reſtytucyon without counſyll whiche vpon ſholde gyuen ¶ foloweth offyce ony thynge temporall ſpyrytuall aperteynynge vnto offyce benefyce ſynned mortally oftentymes hym endeuoured excecute whiche aperteyned vnto ſayd offyce benefyce yf hath made prayer hymſelfe choſen receyued vnto ſayd offyce ſymonyacle yf hath paccyon couenaūt dyſpence aperteyned vnto ye pope y• dyſpence holdeth theuyſhly offyce dygnyte yf ſuffre dyſſymule ony grete ylle ſubgectes may ryght purge correcte deedly ſynne yf hath fauoured ony ayenſt juſtyce vnto dāmage yf hath loſt waſted goodes ye chirche folyſſhe vſages yf hath rebelled ayenſt reaſon vnto ſoueraynes alſo yf hath ben neclygent gete good ſuffycyent counſeyll ſeche juſtyce whiche defaute partye hath ben dāmage theſe thynges dedely ſynne alſo yf hath put offycers indygne vnworthy ſpecyally cure ſoules man knoweth ſouerayne theſe condycyons ſhall togyder concurrentes ſhall conſtrayned gyue ſentence theſe thyngꝭ alledged approued falſely ayenſt hym whiche innocent ſo doynge offyce ſynned may haue meryte opynyon holdeth mayſter fraūces de maronis ſaynt thomas rycharde de villa noua holden ye contrarye affermynge yt juge ſholde ſooner ſuffre deth gyue ſuche ſentence ne conſente ye fyrſte opynyon cauſe pecuniarie y• ſeconde cauſe deth mutilacōn leſe ye goodes fortune oftyme y• grete prouffyte ſoule y• holy ſcrypture whiche may lye forbydeth ſymply deth hym ye whiche innocent lyke wyſe appyred exodi theſe thynges beforſayd prelate prynces juges appyred trouth ſcrypture ye whiche ſayth jugement ryght meruayllos ſhall gyuen vnto y• whiche preceden vnderſtande yf kepe ye lygne purete juſtyce equyte therfore ought fere humyle god juge juges hynge kyngꝭ euery creature moche y• hath ye grete charyte ſeygnourye juſtyce ſayen theſe ſcryptures holy doctrynes yt hath gyuen example bleſſyd ſone god fader jheſus nazarenus ordynarye juge deed quyke therfore whan man wolde take hym make conſtytute hym kynge fledde moūtayne praye vnto god fader whan man hym ſought juge put hym vnto deth hym yelded preſented vnto towne vnto place knowe wel men hym ſholde cauſe deye lyke wyſe wolde ſaye example moche joyouſly ſholde many receyue deth prelacyon offyce benefyce ſeygnourye occaſyon ſeygnourye ſpecyally theſe aduocatꝭ ben ſuche cō dycyon yt offyce aduocate vnto defended ryght cuſtome ſholde thoſe yt ben excōmunycate heretykes religyous theyr monaſterye cōmaūdement lycence theyr prelate ſuche people whiche myſhere aduocacyer ſynnen gretely alſo done ye whiche vnto yt receyuen wyttyngly holy ordres leſſe wt benefyce hȳ enterdyte ye aduocacyer laye courte except owne cauſe chirche caſe pyte ye cauſe yt ben poore alſo juge may aduocacyer cauſe yt ought juge alſo aduocate beuefyced ony chirche may ye ryght aduocacyer ayenſt chirche wtout ſome whiche ſholde ſayd chirche yf h • otherwyſe wyttynge may mortall ſynne reaſon ye contemnement aduocate procurour ſuſtaynen wyttyngly cauſe vniuſte mortall ſȳne holden reſtore vnto ye partye dāmage whiche vnto hym cometh cauſe induce partye yt ſuſteyned reſtore dede ryally enterpryſe ſuſtayne cauſe yt byleued ſomwhat good juſte procedynge knowed fals ought incontynent ceſſe ſhewynge trouth vnto partye aduerſarye vnto hym whome hath pleated inducynge hym apoynte partye yf coūſeyll ayde partye endāmaged leſeth cauſe ye whiche good juſte holden make reſtytucōn enduce hȳ whome ſuſtayned cauſe yt durynge yt cauſe doubtfull man may ſuſtayne pleate wtout ſynne pleatynge hach cōmytte falſy te producynge fals wytneſſes conſented yt hath coūſeylled partye lye alledge thynge whiche fals ayded falſely lawes whiche purpoſe alſo probacōns ye waye ryght de de hath ſought dylacōns cauyllacōns ayen ryght gyue coſtes vexacōns ye partye cauſe ye whiche juſte yf hath appeled juſte ſentēs wyttȳgly al theſe caſe may haue mortall ſynne hath ben ſlouthfull ſtudye ſuſteyne kepe ye good cauſe defaute ſlouth y• partye hath ben dāmage may haue mortall ſynne boūde make reſtytucōn hath ſhewed enalycyouſly ye ſecrete partye ye partye aduerſarye yt whiche cometh coſtes damagꝭ mortall ſȳne ought make reſtytucōn hath loſt ye good cauſe neclygence vnfaythfulnes vycyous ignoraūce holden reſtore ye dāmages whiche cauſe yt cometh ye partye ſee knowe poore peple may purſue defende theyr good cauſe moche ben poore ſeeth yt none vnto gyueth ſocour ye whiche thynge may well ſynned mortally yf vnto wolde yt man dyde vnto hȳ caas ſemblable lawe charyte haue taken excelſyue ſalarye may haue mortall ſynne ſalarye may juged exceſſyue competent cauſe ye labour faconde aduocate alſo ye cuſtome contracte may make couenaūt pryce wt hȳ theaug xiiij q v non ſane whiche vnto hym toke y• cauſe yt cauſe cōmenced yt fynyed yt cōmenced hangynge ryght ſo ſayen ye ryghtes lawfull make couenaūt aduocate haue tenneth hondreth partye determyned oonly ye pryce named certayne ony lawyer gyue counſeyll onyiij q vij fame ſſ p̄terra cauſe yt whiche knoweth vniuſte may wonne ſynned mortally yf ſo happen boūde reſtore ye partye ſayd ye aduocate alſo yf preſented ſage experte ryghtꝭ cuſtomes ye whiche ſcyence hath y• whiche hath gyuen coūſeyll whiche hath borne dāmage vnto partye yf hath demaūded pryce exceſſyue gyue coūſeyll hath coūſeylled ye poore yt ſeeth neceſſyte ſayd aduocate alſo vnto theſe procurours yt vndſtande yf haue procured wyttyngly fals cauſe neclygence hath lette loſe good yf hath gyuen ayde comforte poore yf hath ben exceſſyue ſalarye ſayd aduocate alſo vnto bayllyfes notaryes yf hath done treaſon offyce falſefyenge good lettre wyllynge ſhewe lettres certaynes regyſtres hath wylled teche lyke wyſe ſholde hath taught yt ſholde hath ben ignoraūt regeſtre endyte whiche cometh often proceſſe debate whiche partyes rennen grete dāmages hath ben neclygent ſlouthfull ſpede yelde actes theſe thynges may haue mortall ſynne holden reſtore dāmages whiche ben come defaute hath paſſed teſtamentes thoſe dyſpoſycyon power make teſta ment ben thoſe whiche haue vſaūce reaſon lettynge lawfull mortall ſynne holden dyſdāmage partye hath kept ye ſolemnyte requyſyte wytneſſes othes theſe thynges whiche ben ryght breketh othe ſȳned mortally ouer holden reſtore ye dāmages folowen paſſe without neceſſyte ſuffycyante may haue mortall ſynne hath ſpoken wryten ſtatutes ayenſt lybertees chirche ouer mortall ſȳne excōmunycate notarye byſſhop waged ſuffycyantly yt wt ſtandynge taketh offyce dygnyte chirche well ſayd ſcolers ben excōmunycate alſo ſo euer doctour yt receyued wyttyngly relygyous yt whiche hath lycence prclate excōmunycate alſo yf hath made paccyon rede ſuche wyſe man vnto hȳ ſhall gyue chaūtrye ſymonyacle man may ordeyne yt chaūtrye y• whiche ſholde vacante ſhall haue forth ſuche charge whiche ſhall haue ſhalbe boūde rede alſo yf man enſure yf man promytte whā mā ought make reſtytu • ōn vnto fourth whiche knowe whan man holden reſtore vnderſtande lawfull reteyne frō houre ne moment whan vnto whome ought make reſtytucyon wolde juſtely yt ſayd reſtytucyon vnto hym made allo y• withholder hath place tyme ſpace puyſſaū ce ſhall well lawfull ſome circūſtaunces dyfferre make reſtytucyon whan vnto whome ought made wolde ſholde wyll good reaſon dyfferred moche ſholde vnto grete preiudyce comen wele example whiche ſholde warre ſeruyce kynge whiche hath dyſtreſſed ony lawfull marchaunde ſōme hondred crownes whiche may reſtored without ſellynge hors harneys armes whiche ſhall vnprouffytable vnto welthe comon people reſtytucyon may occaſyon ryght grete ylle royalme defaute one nayle man leſeth ſhoe ſhoe horſe horſe man man bataylle bataylle royalme whiche appyreth marchaunde ſholde loue reſtytucyon dyfferred greate comon welth owne wyll accomplyſſhed lytell welth partyculer therfore ſuche caas ſemblable may well dyfferre reſtytucyon purpoſe reſtore place tyme alſo reſtytucyon may ſomtyme vnto grete peryll dāmage hym vnto whome done glayne man houre fury wolde kylle alſo ſome may ſuche condycyon yf reſtored vpon ye houre ſholde renne grete ſhame grete dāmage vnto whome ſholde make reſtytucyon nothyng lytel profyte ſholde haue ye whiche appyred yt charyte reaſon ought attende place tyme oportunyte reſtytucyon vnto hym made good charyte reaſon lyke wyſe apperteyned theſe thynges beforſayd appyred ynough yt yf thynge wt holden hath ben taken ſecretly ought yelde ſecretly vnto hym ye whiche hath power reſtore vnto hym ſuffyſed vnto ſaluacyon haue dyſpleaſure caas purpoſe yelde many tymes often ſhall haue oportunyte ſayd may reteyne neceſſyte corporell drynke meete cloth lyue delycyouſly holde grete eſtate haboūdaūce mannes goodes ony extreme neceſſyte whiche ſholde take ony thynge fruytefully ayde hym ſuche neceſſyte ſhall holden yelde notwtſtandynge afterwarde hath well power yf hath taken ſuche neceſſyte whiche falleth afterwarde durynge tyme neceſſyte ſhall holden reſtore afterwarde yf haue power ſhall boūde reſtore woman maryed conceyue huſbonde y• caas ſtronge remedye yt may come grete ylle dāmage well vnto huſbonde ye enherytours ye foloweth woman may recouer ſaluacyon yf ſhe make reſtytucyon y• maner many grete theologyens lawyer determen dyuerſely scotte opynyon ſuche woman holden declare herſelf neyther vnto childe ought ſhewe dyſcretly ſone doughter put hym eſtate chirche leue herytage vnto yf ſhe may vnto come ſhe ryche meouables herytages ſhe ought declare b • teſtament wyſe recompenſe moche huſbonde whiche hath charge auoutrye alſo enherytours ſhe may goodly raymonde ſayth yf ſemblable ſuche infante fered loued god perſuaſyble moder myght make ſuche proceſſe vnderſtande confeſſour moder childe hauynge age dyſcrecyon ſholde preſent confeſſour make childe ſwere ſhall holde ſecrete thynge vnto hym wyll declare vnto prouffyte ſoule alſo make moder ſwere ſhe ſhall ſaye without ony malyce trouth theſe thyngꝭ done y• ſayd mod may well ſwere yf ſhe well certayne yt ſayd infante huſbonde ye whiche thynge alwayes y• ſayd infant boūde byleue ſuche maner yt boūde forſake herytage yf byleue forſake dooth well merytoryouſly hath wylled ſaye yf woman huſbonde ſuche condycyons ſhe alſo gouernoureſſe vnto hȳ ſemblable yt ſhe hym ſholde pacyfye ſurete conſcyence ſhe myght declare manyfeſte ouer remedye y• caas beſt yt ſholde poſſyble theſe thynges ſayd appyred gyue true ſure remedye caas thynge ryght harde conſyderynge varyacōns ye circūſtaunces dyuerſe condycyons perſones appyred alſo ye horrybyly te ye ſynne brekynge maryage ye grete theeft dampnacōn many • ybaudes men woman ony lette draweth backe entre good relygyon approued wtout juſte cauſe reſonable ſynned mortally ony vyolence perſone late entred religyon ouer mortall ſynne excōmunycate ſo boūde enduce perſone hath withdrawen myſcoūſeylled entre ſayd relygyon caas may make ſuche induccyon ſholde entre hymſelf yf haue lettynge ſuffycyent lawfull elles maketh reſtytucyon ſuffycyent vnto relygyon haue letted ony come vnto benefyce chirche vnto maryage vnto purchaſe herytage thynge pryncypally anoye hym pryncypally ſynguler prouffyte wt yt awaytynge anoye ſuche condycōn yt hath done ye ſayd lettynge anoye boūde reſtore arbytracyon people reaſon good conſcyence yf haue letted intencyon wyll anoye hym prouffyte hym nothȳ ge holden reſtore euery man may procure prouffyte wayes meanes lawfull honeſte notwithſtondynge occaſyon cometh ſome lettynge dāmage vnto neygh bour yf hath ſtolen lytell hogge ony lytell valour houre hym taketh afterwarde hym nouryſſheth tyll vnto valoure ony grete ſomme holden dede conſcyence reſtore onely vnto valour beſte tyme hym toke alyke thynge ſholde colte beeſtes haue helyd nouryſſhed elles better thynge ſtolen rauyſſhed thynge contrary yf thynge ſtolen impeyred ought repayre ſo holden dāmages whiche may comen vnto hym vnto whome aperteyneth thynge ſtolen cauſe ſayd theft • alſo yf ſuche thynge ſtolen peryſſhe fortune ellys yf abyde alwayes whiche hath ſtolen bounde yf hath done deuoyre offre reſtytucyon thynge peryſſhe whiche reſtytucyon endāmaged hath wyll receyue yf hath boughte wyttyngly thynge ſtolen rauyſſhed whiche wyſe aperteyneth vnto ſeller hath intencyon bye retayne hym ſelfe ouer mortall ſynne holden reſtore vnto hym vnto whome apertayneth thynge ſo bought vnto inherytours vnto poore hath ben ſayd without power repute pryſe hath gyuen onely vnto hym hym hath made ſuche ſale alſo ouer holden kepe harmeles warande hym vnto whome appertayneth thynge ſtolen ſoo euer become yf boughte good intencyon knowe yelde vnto loſte may juſtly repute ſomme gyuen yelde alonely ſurplus may worth yf fynde hym vnto whome ſuche thynge appertyneth yt ſōme ſurplus ought gyuen vnto pore yf hath bought thynge whiche hath ben ſtolen whiche byleueth loyalte holden reſtore tyll vnto certefyed trouth duely certefyed holden reſtore durynge tyme byleueth thynge loyalte peryſſheth conſumed parte bounde reſtore alonely party fruytes hath tyme byleued thynge ſolde truely alſo eten drynken rauen thefte bē holden reſtore vnto eſtymacyon haue taken excepte thoſe whiche ben grete neceſſyte vnto whome may ſemblable ſhall pleaſe well thoſe vnto whome ye ſayd thynge rauyſſhed ſtolen appertayneth ſholde prechers whiche entende enduce theſe theuys amendement vnto reſtytucyon alſo wyſe y• chyldren ſeruaūtes thoſe whiche haue theyr goodes thefte vſury ſymony rauen ben holdē reſtore valour y• may haue ſayd thefte drynke meete hoſe cloth otherwyſe onely moche haue laboured take payne ammonycion wyſe reſtytucyon made vnto partye alſo yf goodes whiche euyll goten hath ſome whiche truely goten may adreſſe theyr intencyon lyue thoſe goodes thefte may lyue wt theyr laboure ſholde demaūde prouyſyon juſtyce yf may lyue ony wayes ſayd ſholde ſooner demaū de almes lyue thefte nedyll nother lytell thynge wyll weyed god werke outwarde yf hath taken theuyſſhly y• godes hym whiche vnto hym oweth ony ſomme tyll vnto pryce dette leſſe good cōſcyence conſyderynge ouer well paye hym without plee lettynge maner yll ſynne fere god pacyence dāmage may purchaſe grete meryte neuertheles ſuche caſe holden bounde reſtore hym ouer ſome ſayen yf ſuche maner takynge theuyſſhely ſentence excomunycate caſte whiche hath taken ſayd acurſyd holy chirche intendeth bynde ſuche ſentence thoſe witholdeth fro another agayne reaſon malycyouſly whiche thynge doth whiche payed ſayd notwithſtondynge lawe ciuyle ſholde culpable punyſſhed foloweth falleth ſayd ſentence ſholde take hede vnto whome ſuche caſe ſholde come gyue doynge ſclaunder euyll example vnto neyghbours yf offycer take gyftes ſeruyces pleſer vnto ony vnto preiudyce juſtyce dammage another deedly ſynne alſo yf thretenynges otherwyſe extorcyoneth gyftes promyſſes journey thynge notable ought reſtore payne ſome pleaſure done reſonably may receyue vnto hym ſhall gyue lyberally theſe lordes chirch ſecularyte may receyue amendes yt ben taxed theyr courtes ryght good cuſtome ſoo done hate couetyſe curſyd occaſyon good counſeyll departe ſuche amendes vnto power ſpecyall whan amendes ſurmonteth dāmage yf hath vſyd wyttyngly thynge lent ouer termes wyll lener ſynneth mortally holden make ſatyſfaccyon yf thynge lente impeyre loſte holden reſtore yf hath lente wyttyngly ony thynge tonne muſty put wyne horſe another thynge whiche cometh dāmage vnto hym whiche borowed lener holden kepe hym harmeles alſo whiche hyred wynne journey ony werke ye whiche vndertaketh carye tōnes wyne voweth thynge holden reſtore dā mages whiche cometh vnto ſayd werke defaute notellys yf haue taken kepe ony thynge ought yelde excepte ſome caſe fyrſte whan ſhall yelde vnto grete yl dāmage hym vnto whome man ſholde yelde ſholde yelde glayue vnto man furyous ſeconde whan thefe hath gyuen kepe thefte man ſholde yelde ſooner vnto lorde thyrde whan gyuer ſholde forfayte whiche goodes ſhold lyke wyſe forfayte nother maner y• whiche taketh kepe ought reſtore thynge peryſſhe loſſe defaute caſe fortune yf take ſalarye kepynge yf vnto bounde yelde terme ſholde yelde rule generall mater vnderſtonde thynge lente put kepynge hyred abyde vnto peryll hym whiche gyueth yf bergayne made bytwene gyuer receyuer gylte defaute hym whiche receyueth longe abydynge alſo euery man holden reſtore hath receyued bequeſte ony playe thoſe whiche hath loſte theyr wyttes naturall ben waſters chyldern faderles moderles yonge folke vnder yeres xxv whiche frāneſye dcef dōme blynde ſyknes perpetuall theſe ſayd proprely lordes theyr goodes maner may alyen without ordynaūce vnto whome appertayneth ordenarely lyke wyſe ſeruy tour chylde whiche houſholde gouernaunce fader woman maryed monke whiche hath admynyſtracyon goodes chirche thoſe y• whiche haue rente benefyces chirche theſe maner people may juſtely alyen goodes whiche ben ſubiectes theyr ſouerayns agayne juſte wyll reſonable mayſter good man houſe huſbonde abbot pope theſe whiche wyttyngly receyuen vnduely ſuche maner perſones ben holden make reſtytucyon alſo thoſe wynnen playes dyſe cardys ben holden reſtore whan curſyd couetyſe fraudes force importunyte haue enducyd theyr partye playe haue made decepcyon maner playe another thynge ſholde playe fordyſporte recreacyon playes honeſte defended ſome lytell thynges condycyons perſones dyner y• ſouper amonge lordes ryche people whiche attende dyſporte recreacyon gayns y• loſſe ſuche caſe ſhal fall reſtytucyon put may haue venyall ſynne alſo noted pyllers rauyſſhars goodes whiche pyllers ben knowen publyſſhed whiche hath ben warnyd duely reſtore haue wyl whan ſholde may yf ſuche eſtate comen vnto dethe wolde well make reſtytucyon may ſholde buryed halowed grounde notwithſtondynge haue ben aſſoyled receyued body oure lorde alſo thoſe whiche receyuen gyftes knowen well done fere loue gyuers ben deceyued wenynge gyue vnto one gyuen vnto another yf ony myſthynkynge fyccyon hym calleth kynnyſman ony affermeth poore indygent ſo ben many trewandes dronken beggers whiche oftymes demaunden almes receyuen many whiche ben nedy ben alſo ſuche maner people ben holden make reſtytucyon gyuers ben cōſtrayned fere loſſe deceyued ignoraunce whiche foloweth whiche gyuen proprely gyuen euery gyfte ought procede pryncypally fontayne loue alſo theſe whiche maken edefyen waremes douue houſes vnto grete dāmage preiudyce hys neyghbour wyll repayre y• dāmage y• whyche foloweth ſynnen mortally weremes douue houſes auncyent ſome ſayen whan ſēblable yt kepe herytage ner heſt neyghbours ben caſte vnder moche holden theyr herytages leſſe pryce good cauſe lordes theſe douue howres theſe waremes holdē reſtore alſo thoſe whiche holden nouryſſhe beſtes noyous ſholde wulfe bere dogge whiche byteth ye people eſtrangleth ony fame beeſtes oxe whiche ſtryketh horne ben holden repayre dāmages preceptum no ordinat ad reueren • iam veritatis ſummeideo non debimus ſine cauſa iurarealexander de hal tercio bonaucn̄ tercio idem vbi ſupra idem nicolaus de lyra matheiv capitlo idē ibidem reuerenter eſt ad ocultū dei ſi irreuerenter eſt opoſitum jurare ſine cauſa et vtilicate eſt porcio irreuerēcie veritatis diuine juracio nominis dei vbi nulla eſt neceſſitas vel vtilitas valde eſt irreprehenſibilis juramentum incautum quod fit ſine cauſa vel neceſſitate importat irreuerenciam diuini nominis non ſolum iuramentum mendax ſed eciam quod fit ſine neceſſitate et vtilitate eſt ſecundo precepto inibitum jurare ſine cauſa eſt nomen dei vanū aſſumere diſponit hominē ad conceptū dei non eſt iurandum de falſo nec de mutili et non eciam niſi de iuſticia et veritate iuramentum debet eſſe diſcreta deliberacio vt non iuretur verum niſi pro neceſſitate vel vtilitate ex irreuerencia naſcitur iurandi conſuetudo que peccatum eſt iugens et mortale et non ſolū vnum ſed multiplex prayſe whiche ſuche gyfte benefyce yelden vnto creatoure ſeconde redempcyon humayne lygnage y• bleſſyd ſeen clerely manyfeſtly loue infynyte god vnto hath ſhewed bleſſyd carnacyon ryght pyteous paſſyon whiche hath delyuered eternall dampnacyon gyuen grace prayſynges vocales melodyous vnto redemp • ſoo moche excellently mortall man ne may ſpeke worthely thyrde benedyccyon grace dyuyne whiche mercy infynyte hath worſhypped ouercome worlde oftentymes hath called agayne releued preſerued grete deteſtable ſynnes wel myſterye ſacramentes holy chirche alſo g • uynge kepynge ſeruyce bleſſyd angelles cour • e celeſtyall whiche grace benefyces ſaued knowen ryght well perfectly whiche gyuen prayſe vnto god inceſſably fourth glorye vnto whiche ſeen come ben certayne ſhall neuer leſſe ſhall neuer defayle neyther body ne ſoule • ut ben ſhall dwelle eternyte pea loue force beaute youth goodes grete infynyte ony herte ne may thynke ryght gloryous companye ryght gloryous royalme ryght delectable lyf felycyte infynyte none ſuffycyant vnderſtande wryte nombre comprehende theſe thynges beforeſayd notwithſtandynge ben grete meruaylle playnely ben leſſe thynge comparyſon ryall veryte ryght lytell droppe dewe regarde y• water god hath create therfore better ceſſe ſo moche wryte hym retorne vnto deugute oryſon without whiche none ought ony thynge begynne lyke wyſe ende true god mercy pea conſolacyon fontayne loue pyte ſwetnes lyght infynyte lyf eternall vnto yelde dygne cruell deth depnes ignoraūce myſery welth aſſured indygne ſpeke beſechynge ryght humbly may pleaſe gyue taſte felynge preſentlyf paynes helle joyes parady ſe ye haue gyuen grace ſpeke preſent treatyſe wryte vnto may fere redoubte fynally myne herte loue creatoure heuen erthe whiche ryght juſtely gyueſt helle vnto dampned bleſſyd paradyſe vnto ſaued confeſſe aduowe haytyf ſynner whiche goodes body ſoule hath ryght folyſſhely dyſpended vnworthy lyfte vp face ayenſt ſonne mone wt ſtandynge god fader pyteous euery creature fontayne mercy ryght juſtely requyre ayde court celeſtyall ryght ſyngulerly virgyne gloryous moder ſouerayne lorde • rpnes grace 〈…〉 ne aduocate ſynners ende theyr interceſſyons nere dyſprayſed ryght dampnably treſpaſſed whiche thynge mooſt grete exces dolorous pyte may ymagyued foloweth almooſt worlde whiche reygned theſe ryght peryllous daūgerous dayes go vnto perdycyon conſyderacyon whiche exces hath cauſe motyue compoſycyon preſent booke conſolacyon reuocacyon ſymple people ende thoſe whiche wyll rede may conſyder haue auouwed vnto holy baptem alſo vnderſtande trought cōmaundementes god werkes mercy whiche knowlege may correcte purefye theyr ſynnes holy entyere confeſſyon fere redoubte horryble paynes helle ferme hope mowe come vnto ryght gloryous company
